```dafny
// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanForm...

```dafny
// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {

    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}
```

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

```dafny
// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {

    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1...

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}
```

// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      // Suppose for contradiction that CanFormGoodOfLength holds
      // Then there exists numA such that 0 <= numA <= k,
      // numA <= CountA(s), and 2 * numA > k
      // But k >= 2 * count and numA <= CountA(s) = count,
      // so 2 * numA <= 2 * count <= k, contradiction.
      // We formalize this reasoning:
      var numA := 0;
      // We need to show that for any numA satisfying the constraints,
      // 2 * numA <= k.
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])
}

ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    assert forall k | candidate < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) :: 2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

{

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k > candidate;
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      // Assume for contradiction that CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k) holds
      // Then there exists numA with 0 <= numA <= k, numA <= CountA(s),
      // and 2 * numA > k. From 2 * numA > k >= 2 * count we get numA > count.
      // But count = CountA(s), so numA > CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s).
      // Thus CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k) cannot hold.
      // Formalize the contradiction:
      assert exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) && 2 * numA > k;
      // Let that numA witness be `v`.
      var v := witness;
      assert 0 <= v <= k;
      assert v <= CountA(s);
      assert 2 * v > k;
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert 2 * v > 2 * count;
      assert v > count;
      assert count == CountA(s);
      assert v > CountA(s);
      // This contradicts v <= CountA(s).
    }
  }
}

  if |s| < candidate {

    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;

    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }

// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])

ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      // For any numA that satisfies the bounds, prove 2*numA <= k
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?

// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).

{

  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len

  if |s| == 0 then 0

ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])

// Can we form a "good" subsequence of exactly `len` characters from `s`?
// A good string has strictly more than half its characters equal to 'a'.
// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).
ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k
          by {
            // Since 2 * numA > k is impossible, assume otherwise:
            assert 2 * numA > k => False;
          };
    }
  }
}

{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {

    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

// Count the number of 'a' characters in a string
ghost function CountA(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{

  else (if s[|s|-1] == 'a' then 1 else 0) + CountA(s[..|s|-1])

// We choose numA of the available 'a's and (len - numA) of the available non-'a's,
// such that 2 * numA > len (the "good" condition).

{

  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len

  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

ghost predicate CanFormGoodOfLength(s: string, len: int)
{
  0 <= len <= |s| &&
  exists numA: int | 0 <= numA <= len ::
    numA <= CountA(s) &&
    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&
    2 * numA > len
}

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

  0 <= len <= |s| &&

    len - numA + CountA(s) <= |s| &&

lemma CountABound(s: string)
  ensures CountA(s) <= |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountABound(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

method LoveA(s: string) returns (result: int)
  requires CountA(s) >= 1
  ensures 0 <= result <= |s|
  ensures CanFormGoodOfLength(s, result)
  ensures forall k | result < k <= |s| :: !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
{
  CountABound(s);

  var count := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant count == CountA(s[..i])
  {
    if s[i] == 'a' {
      count := count + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert count == CountA(s);

  var candidate := 2 * count - 1;
  if |s| < candidate {
    result := |s|;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= |s|;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    // Witness for CanFormGoodOfLength: numA = count
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}

    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert |s| - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > |s|;
    // Maximality: range result < k <= |s| is empty since result == |s|
  } else {
    result := candidate;
    assert 0 <= count <= candidate;
    assert count <= CountA(s);
    assert candidate - count + CountA(s) <= |s|;
    assert 2 * count > candidate;

    // Prove maximality: for k > 2*count-1, any numA with 2*numA > k
    // requires numA > count = CountA(s), contradicting numA <= CountA(s)
    forall k | candidate < k <= |s|
      ensures !CanFormGoodOfLength(s, k)
    {
      assert k >= 2 * count;
      assert forall numA: int | 0 <= numA <= k && numA <= CountA(s) ::
        2 * numA <= k;
    }
  }
}
